< text>
I really appreciated the combination of professionalism and compassion that our cat was given during an emergency visit to Animal Urgent Care. Unfortunately, our cat had a serious health issue that resulted in her needing to be put to sleep but everyone at Animal Urgent Care made it very clear to me that the pet's comfort was the number one priority. Dr. Berman was clear, thoughtful and patient through the whole process...she made a difficult decision much easier. Additionally, while I have been gouged at other emergency vets, Animal Urgent Care charged me significantly less than what I agreed to after the first tests suggested that the condition was already very advanced. I would not hesitate to take another pet here under any conditions, they're wonderful people.</text>

<user>111044351134002538272</user>< Name>
Ser3nity Now<//Name>
<Time>1604786613724</Time><rate>3</rate>< review>
I'm very torn about my experience here a few days ago… I have a lot of experience w/ vets & animal care, & believe that Dr. Linney is a very kind & knowledgeable vet who cares for the health and safety of the animals he treats. Other than suggesting a culture on my dog's bite wound to help pinpoint what antibiotic is best (which is an understandable suggestion, but not necessary at that point in my opinion) he didn't use scare tactics to sell unnecessary treatments, vaccines, or medications like so many other vets I've been to have tried. The rest of the staff were all extremely friendly & attentive to me & my dog's needs as well.

With that being said, the problem I have are the inflated prices for care…. My dog needed an exam, laceration repair requiring a few stitches, light sedation ("2 glasses of wine sedation" not fully put under sedation), local anesthetic, antibiotics, & pain medication. I was quoted $765 - $1,072 for his treatment. I had to decline bc it was too expensive, so I just ended up paying $162 for the exam, a bandage, about 4 day's worth of pain meds, & no antibiotics.

The original quote said antibiotics & pain meds would be $150 total, but after I declined treatment, they wanted to send me home with antibiotics for $159 & pain meds for $32. Why did the price for both go up to $191 from $150?

I ended up going to the original vet I wanted to go to after convincing them to make time for me, which they were kind enough to eventually figure out. I paid $515 for everything, which included anti-inflammatories as well as antibiotics & pain meds.

Overall, the staff is very kind, caring, & knowledgeable, but their prices are over-inflated "nickel & dime" charges. I've been to much worse vets who over charge as well as scare worried or unknowledgeable clients into paying for things they don't need, so this office isn't at the bottom of my list (I was quoted $1,200 by two other vets, but the other 18 I called that day wouldn't even give me a rough estimate) & there's only one vet in the LA area that I could find so far with reasonable pricing, but their wait times are long w/ limited hours of operation.

If you do go here, I'm sure you'll get quality care, but just be prepared for the prices.

I also recommend, depending on the severity of your situation, trying to learn as much as you can about treatment &/or care requirements for your pet before going to any vet clinic so that you don't get talked into unnecessary vaccines, prescription food, tests, &/or treatment…. It is very important to do your own research. Also, ask the vet questions, especially in terms of what is 100% needed for treatment & why, as well as what suggestions they made aren't needed, but why they suggested them in the first place. You can make better decisions this way.< /review>

Great for bluegill if you have children. The hatchery trout have parasites, so be wary. The largemouth bass are very leader shy. All in all, an excellent place to bring the family. Combustion motors are not allowed, but you can bring an electric motor. Most people just bring kayaks and oars.< /Review>

< Review>
We are so happy that McRoskey Mattress Co. still exists! Yesterday we went  to look at options for a new mattress.  Our 20 yr McRoskey had served us well, but it was time for a new mattress. Our first experience with McRoskey was 24 years ago when we were looking for a custom mattress/boxspring for our toddler daughter's antique bed.  Mr. McRoskey came out to our house himself to measure.   Another daughter later and more mattresses, we couldn't imagine sleeping on anything else. So, reading about the business changes, we were a little worried.  However, Eyreka and Marina could not have been more helpful. Their only interest was in helping us choose a mattress best for us.  It is this kind of customer service that we have come to appreciate from this terrific family business.  Eyreka and Marina represent the company well.  Thank you.< /Review>

< review>
I wanted to get back into golfing after not playing for years but didn’t want to spend too much money on a set of clubs. I was lucky enough to walk in and meet the owner Glenn who is a friendly guy and seemed to be happy to see another person trying to get into (or back into) golf. The store has both new and used clubs and Glenn helped me pick out some used clubs and gave them new handles that feel comfortable in my hands.

At the end of the day, I got myself a new bag, 1 driver, 1 wood, a set of Calloway irons, a putter, towel, glove, 6 golf balls, and a handful of tees for $420, after a discount thanks to Glenn! He also gave me a 30 day satisfaction guarantee so if I do not like the clubs I can come back and I believe trade it in or get my money back, however I may have forgotten the actual details regarding this haha.

I definitely recommend this place for people who are trying to pick up this hobby!</review>
